[];\n        let approvals = [];\n\n        // Tab Switching\n        function switchTab(tabName) {\n            document.querySelectorAll(\'.tab-button\').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove(\'active\'));\n            document.querySelectorAll(\'.tab-content\').forEach(content => content.classList.remove(\'active\'));\n            \n            event.target.classList.add(\'active\');\n            document.getElementById(`tab-${tabName}`).classList.add(\'active\');\n        }\n\n        // Terminal Logging\n        function addLog(message, type = \'info\') {\n            const terminal = document.getElementById(\'terminal-output\');\n            const line = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            line.className = `terminal-line ${type}`;\n            const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n            line.textContent = `[${timestamp}] ${message}`;\n            terminal.appendChild(line);\n            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;\n        }\n\n        function clearTerminal() {\n            document.getElementById(\'terminal-output\').innerHTML = \'\';\n            addLog(\'Terminal cleared\', \'info\');\n        }\n\n        // Modal Functions\n        function showInitModal() {\n            document.getElementById(\'init-modal\').classList.add(\'active\');\n        }\n\n document.getElementById(\'magnify-modal\').classList.add(\'active\');\n        }\n\n        function closeMagnifyModal() {\n            document.getElementById(\'magnify-modal\').classList.remove(\'active\');\n        }\n\n        // System Initialization\n        async function initializeSystem() {\n            const mode = document.getElementById(\'init-mode\').value;\n            const context = document.getElementById(\'init-context\').value;\n\n            addLog(`Initializing system in ${mode} mode...`, \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/initialize`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({ mode, context })\n                });\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                if (data.success) {\n                    addLog(`✓ System initialized in ${mode} mode`, \'success\');\n                    closeInitModal();\n                    updateStatus();\n                } else {\n                    addLog(`✗ Initialization failed: ${data.message}`, \'error\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Document Management\n        async function createDocument() {\n            const title = document.getElementById(\'doc-title\').value.trim();\n            const content = document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value.trim();\n            const type = document.getElementById(\'doc-type\').value;\n\n            if (!title || !content) {\n                addLog(\'✗ Title and content are required\', \'error\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            addLog(`Creating document: ${title}...`, \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/documents`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({ title, content, type })\n                });\n\n                const doc = await response.json();\n                documents[doc.id] = doc;\n                currentDocId = doc.id;\n                \n                addLog(`✓ Document created: ${title}`, \'success\');\n                updateDocumentList();\n                updateStatus();\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error creating document: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        function saveDocument() {\n            if (!currentDocId) {\n                createDocument();\n            } else {\n                addLog(\'Document saved locally\', \'success\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        function clearDocument() {\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-title\').value = \'\';\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value = \'\';\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-type\').value = \'general\';\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-state-display\').textContent = \'New\';\n            currentDocId = null;\n            addLog(\'Document editor cleared\', \'info\');\n        }\n\n        function magnifyDocument() {\n            if (!currentDocId) {\n                addLog(\'✗ No document selected\', \'error\');\n                return;\n            }\n            showMagnifyModal();\n        }\n\n        async function executeMagnify() {\n            const domain = document.getElementById(\'magnify-domain\').value;\n            \n            addLog(`Magnifying document with ${domain} expertise...`, \'info\');\n            closeMagnifyModal();\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/documents/${currentDocId}/magnify`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({ domain })\n                });\n\n                const result = await response.json();\n                \n                if (result.success) {\n                    addLog(`✓ Document magnified with ${domain} expertise`, \'success\');\n                    document.getElementById(\'doc-state-display\').textContent = \'Magnified\';\n                    document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value = result.content || document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value;\n                } else {\n                    addLog(`✗ Magnification failed`, \'error\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function simplifyDocument() {\n            if (!currentDocId) {\n                addLog(\'✗ No document selected\', \'error\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            addLog(\'Simplifying document...\', \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/documents/${currentDocId}/simplify`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }\n                });\n\n                const result = await response.json();\n                \n                if (result.success) {\n                    addLog(\'✓ Document simplified\', \'success\');\n                    document.getElementById(\'doc-state-display\').textContent = \'Simplified\';\n                    document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value = result.content || document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value;\n                } else {\n                    addLog(\'✗ Simplification failed\', \'error\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function solidifyDocument() {\n            if (!currentDocId) {\n                addLog(\'✗ No document selected\', \'error\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            addLog(\'Solidifying document and generating tasks...\', \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/documents/${currentDocId}/solidify`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }\n                });\n\n                const result = await response.json();\n                \n                addLog(\'✓ Document solidified\', \'success\');\n                addLog(`✓ Generated ${result.prompts?.length || 0} prompts`, \'success\');\n                addLog(`✓ Created ${result.tasks?.length || 0} tasks`, \'success\');\n                addLog(`✓ Generated ${result.gates?.length || 0} gates`, \'success\');\n                \n                document.getElementById(\'doc-state-display\').textContent = \'Solidified\';\n                \n                if (result.tasks) tasks = tasks.concat(result.tasks);\n                if (result.gates) gates = gates.concat(result.gates);\n                \n                updateStatus();\n                refreshTasks();\n                refreshGates();\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        function updateDocumentList() {\n            const listEl = document.getElementById(\'document-list\');\n            const docArray = Object.values(documents);\n            \n            if (docArray.length === 0) {\n                listEl.innerHTML = \'<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">📭</div><div>No documents yet</div></div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n\n            listEl.innerHTML = docArray.map(doc => `\n                <div class="document-item ${doc.id === currentDocId ? \'selected\' : \'\'}" onclick="selectDocument(\'${doc.id}\')">\n                    <div class="doc-title">${doc.title}</div>\n                    <div class="doc-meta">Type: ${doc.type}</div>\n                    <div class="doc-state">${doc.state || \'New\'}</div>\n                </div>\n            `).join(\'\');\n        }\n\n        function selectDocument(docId) {\n            const doc = documents[docId];\n            if (!doc) return;\n\n            currentDocId = docId;\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-title\').value = doc.title;\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-content\').value = doc.content;\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-type\').value = doc.type;\n            document.getElementById(\'doc-state-display\').textContent = doc.state || \'New\';\n            \n            updateDocumentList();\n            addLog(`Selected document: ${doc.title}`, \'info\');\n        }\n\n        // Task Management\n        function refreshTasks() {\n            const listEl = document.getElementById(\'task-list\');\n            \n            if (tasks.length === 0) {\n                listEl.innerHTML = \'<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">⚙️</div><div>No tasks yet. Solidify a document to generate tasks.</div></div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n\n            listEl.innerHTML = tasks.map((task, idx) => `\n                <div class="task-item">\n                    <div class="task-info">\n                        <div class="task-title">Task ${idx + 1}: ${task.type || \'General\'}</div>\n                        <div class="task-meta">Swarm:    <button class="button" onclick="executeTask(\'${task.id || idx}\')">▶️ Execute</button>\n                </div>\n            `).join(\'\');\n        }\n\n        async function executeTask(taskId) {\n            addLog(`Executing task ${taskId}...`, \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/tasks/${taskId}/execute`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }\n                });\n\n                const result = await response.json();\n                \n                if (result.success) {\n                    addLog(`✓ Task ${taskId} completed`, \'success\');\n                    \n                    // Update task status\n                    const task = tasks.find(t => t.id === taskId || tasks.indexOf(t) == taskId);\n                    if (task) task.status = \'complete\';\n                    \n                    refreshTasks();\n                    updateStatus();\n                } else {\n                    addLog(`✗ Task execution failed`, \'error\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Gate Management\n        function refreshGates() {\n            const gridEl = document.getElementById(\'gate-grid\');\n            \n            if (gates.length === 0) {\n                gridEl.innerHTML = \'<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">🛡️</div><div>No gates yet. Solidify a document to generate gates.</div></div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n\n            gridEl.innerHTML = gates.map(gate => `\n                <div class="gate-card ${gate.status              <div class="gate-status">${gate.status || \'Active\'}</div>\n                </div>\n            `).join(\'\');\n        }\n\n        // Approval Management\n        async function consolidateApprovals() {\n            addLog(\'Consolidating approvals...\', \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/approvals/consolidate`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks.filter(t => t.status === \'complete\') })\n                });\n\n                const result = await response.json();\n                \n                if (result.consolidated) {\n                    addLog(\'✓ Approvals consolidated\', \'success\');\n                    approvals.push(result);\n                    updateStatus();\n                    refreshApprovals();\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`✗ Error: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        function refreshApprovals() {\n            const listEl = class="empty-state-icon">✋</div><div>No pending approvals</div></div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n\n            listEl.innerHTML = approvals.map((approval, idx) => `\n                <div class="approval-item">\n                    <div class="approval-header">\n                        <div class="approval-title">Approval Request ${idx + 1}</div>\n                        <div approve consolidated tasks\'}</div>\n                </div>\n            `).join(\'\');\n        }\n\n        function approveRequest(idx) {\n            addLog(`✓ Approval ${idx + 1} approved`, \'success\');\n            approvals.splice(idx, 1);\n            refreshApprovals();\n            updateStatus();\n        }\n\n        function rejectRequest(idx) {\n            addLog(`✗ Approval ${idx + 1} rejected`, \'warning\');\n            approvals.splice(idx, 1);\n            refreshApprovals();\n            updateStatus();\n        }\n\n        // Status Updates\n        async function updateStatus() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/status`);\n                const status = await response.json();\n\n                document.getElementById(\'doc-count\').textContent = Object.keys(documents).length;\n                document.getElementById(\'task-count\').textContent = tasks.length;\n                document.getElementById(\'gate-count\').textContent = gates.length;\n                document.getElementById(\'artifact-count\').textContent = status.artifacts || 0;\n document.getElementById(\'overview-tasks\').textContent = tasks.length;\n                document.getElementById(\'overview-gates\').textContent = gates.length;\n                document.getElementById(\'overview-artifacts\').textContent = status.artifacts || 0;\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\'Status update failed:\', error);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Groq Test\n        async function testGroq() {\n            addLog(\'Testing Groq API...\', \'info\');\n\n            try {\n                const response = await Request Analysis → Identify domain gaps\n2. Template Selection → Choose relevant templates\n3. Question Generation → Create domain-specific questions\n4. Knowledge Gathering → Collect information via Q&A\n5. Domain Synthesis → Create custom domain definition\n6. Cross-Impact Analysis → Map to existing domains\n7. System Augmentation → Add to domain taxonomy\n8. Validation → Test with similar requests\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📋 Generative Domain Templates\n\n### Template 1: New Industry Vertical\n```yaml\ndomain_name: "[Industry] Domain"\npurpose: "Specialized requirements for [industry]"\n\ndiscovery_questions:\n  - What are the unique characteristics of this industry?\n  - What are the regulatory requirements specific to this industry?\n  - What are the standard practices in this industry?\n  - What are the key success factors?\n  - What are the common challenges?\n  - What are the industry-specific metrics?\n  - What are the competitive dynamics?\n  - What are the technology requirements?\n\nsub_domains:\n  - [To be filled based on responses]\n\ncross_domain_impacts:\n  business: "[How this affects business strategy]"\n  engineering: "[Technical implications]"\n  financial: "[Financial considerations]"\n  legal: "[Regulatory/compliance issues]"\n  operations: "[Operational requirements]"\n  marketing: "[Market positioning]"\n  hr: "[Talent requirements]"\n  sales: "[Sales approach]"\n  product: "[Product requirements]"\n\nconstraints:\n  - [Industry-specific constraints]\n\ngates:\n  - [Industry-specific validation gates]\n```\n\n### Template 2: Hybrid Domain\n```yaml\ndomain_name: "[Domain A] + [Domain B] Hybrid"\npurpose: "Integration of [A] and [B] requirements"\n\nprimary_domains:\n  - domain_a: "[Primary domain 1]"\n  - domain_b: "[Primary domain 2]"\n\ndiscovery_questions:\n  - How do these domains interact?\n  - What are the integration points?\n  - What are the conflicting requirements?\n  - What are the synergies?\n  - What are the unique challenges of combining these?\n  - What expertise is required?\n  - What are the success criteria?\n  - What are the risks of integration?\n\nintegration_requirements:\n  - [Specific integration needs]\n\nconflict_resolution:\n  - [How to resolve domain conflicts]\n\ncross_domain_impacts:\n  [Map to all existing domains]\n```\n\n### Template 3: Emerging Technology Domain\n```yaml\ndomain_name: "[Technology] Domain"\npurpose: "Leverage [technology] for business value"\n\ntechnology_stack:\n  - [Core technologies]\n\ndiscovery_questions:\n  - What problem does this technology solve?\n  - What are the technical requirements?\n  - What is the maturity level of this technology?\n  - What are the implementation challenges?\n  - What expertise is required?\n  - What are the costs and ROI?\n  - What are the risks?\n  - What are the competitive advantages?\n\nadoption_requirements:\n  - [Technical requirements]\n  - [Skill requirements]\n  - [Infrastructure requirements]\n\ncross_domain_impacts:\n  [Map to all existing domains]\n```\n\n### Template 4: Process Innovation Domain\n```yaml\ndomain_name: "[Process] Innovation Domain"\npurpose: "Novel approach to [process/function]"\n\ninnovation_type:\n  - [Type of innovation]\n\ndiscovery_questions:\n  - What is the current state?\n  - What is the desired future state?\n  - What is the innovation?\n  - What are the benefits?\n  - What are the risks?\n  - What are the implementation requirements?\n  - What are the success metrics?\n  - What are the change management needs?\n\nimplementation_plan:\n  - [Steps to implement]\n\ncross_domain_impacts:\n  [Map to all existing domains]\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🔍 Generative Domain Question Framework\n\n### Phase 1: Domain Identification\n**Questions:**\n1. What is the primary focus of this request?\n2. Does this fit into any existing domain? (Show list)\n3. If not, what makes this unique?\n4. What are the key characteristics?\n5. What industry or field does this relate to?\n\n### Phase 2: Scope Definition\n**Questions:**\n1. What is the scope of this domain?\n2. What are the boundaries?\n3. What is included?\n4. What is excluded?\n5. How does this relate to existing domains?\n\n### Phase 3: Requirements Gathering\n**Questions:**\n1. What are the functional requirements?\n2. What are the technical requirements?\n3. What are the business requirements?\n4. What are the regulatory requirements?\n5. What are the resource requirements?\n6. What are the timeline requirements?\n7. What are the budget requirements?\n8. What are the quality requirements?\n\n### Phase 4: Stakeholder Analysis\n**Questions:**\n1. Who are the key stakeholders?\n2. What are their needs?\n3. What are their constraints?\n4. What are their success criteria?\n5. What are their concerns?\n6. What is their level of involvement?\n\n### Phase 5: Risk Assessment\n**Questions:**\n1. What are the technical risks?\n2. What are the business risks?\n3. What are the financial risks?\n4. What are the legal risks?\n5. What are the operational risks?\n6. What are the market risks?\n7. What are the mitigation strategies?\n\n### Phase 6: Success Criteria\n**Questions:**\n1. What does success look like?\n2. What are the key metrics?\n3. What are the milestones?\n4. What are the deliverables?\n5. What is the timeline?\n6. What are the acceptance criteria?\n\n### Phase 7: Cross-Domain Impact\n**Questions:**\nFor each existing domain:\n1. How does this affect [domain]?\n2. What are the dependencies?\n3. What are the constraints?\n4. What are the opportunities?\n5. What are the risks?\n\n---\n\n## 🔄 Domain Augmentation Process\n\n### Step 1: Request Analysis\n```python\ndef analyze_request(request):\n    # Extract key concepts\n    concepts = extract_concepts(request)\n    \n    # Match against existing domains\n    domain_matches = match_domains(concepts)\n    \n    # Calculate coverage\n    coverage = calculate_coverage(domain_matches)\n    \n    if coverage < 0.7:  # Less than 70% coverage\n        return "GENERATIVE_DOMAIN_NEEDED"\n    else:\n        return domain_matches\n```\n\n### Step 2: Template Selection\n```python\ndef select_template(request, concepts):\n    templates = {\n        \'industry\': Template1_NewIndustry,\n        \'hybrid\': Template2_HybridDomain,\n        \'technology\': Template3_EmergingTech,\n        \'process\': Template4_ProcessInnovation\n    }\n    \n    # Analyze request characteristics\n    if is_industry_specific(request):\n        return templates[\'industry\']\n    elif has_multiple_domains(concepts):\n        return templates[\'hybrid\']\n    elif is_technology_focused(request):\n        return templates[\'technology\']\n    elif is_process_innovation(request):\n        return templates[\'process\']\n    else:\n        return templates[\'hybrid\']  # Default\n```\n\n### Step 3: Question Generation\n```python\ndef generate_questions(template, request):\n    # Start with template questions\n    questions = template.discovery_questions\n    \n    # Add context-specific questions\n    context_questions = generate_context_questions(request)\n    \n    # Add cross-domain questions\n    cross_domain_questions = generate_cross_domain_questions()\n    \n    return questions + context_questions + cross_domain_questions\n```\n\n### Step 4: Interactive Q&A\n```python\ndef conduct_qa_session(questions):\n    responses = {}\n    \n    for question in questions:\n        # Present question to user\n        response = ask_user(question)\n        \n        # Store response\n        responses[question] = response\n        \n        # Generate follow-up questions if needed\n        if needs_clarification(response):\n            followup = generate_followup(question, response)\n            responses[followup] = ask_user(followup)\n    \n    return responses\n```\n\n### Step 5: Domain Synthesis\n```python\ndef synthesize_domain(template, responses):\n    # Fill template with responses\n    domain = template.fill(responses)\n    \n    # Generate sub-domains\n    domain.sub_domains = identify_sub_domains(responses)\n    \n    # Map cross-domain impacts\n    domain.cross_impacts = map_cross_impacts(responses)\n    \n    # Define constraints\n    domain.constraints = extract_constraints(responses)\n    \n    # Generate gates\n    domain.gates = generate_domain_gates(responses)\n    \n    return domain\n```\n\n### Step 6: Validation\n```python\ndef validate_domain(domain):\n    # Check completeness\n    completeness = check_completeness(domain)\n    \n    # Check consistency\n    consistency = check_consistency(domain)\n    \n    # Check cross-domain impacts\n    impacts_valid = validate_cross_impacts(domain)\n    \n    if completeness and consistency and impacts_valid:\n        return True\n    else:\n        return identify_gaps(domain)\n```\n\n### Step 7: System Integration\n```python\ndef integrate_domain(domain):\n    # Add to domain taxonomy\n    add_to_taxonomy(domain)\n    \n    # Update cross-domain mappings\n    update_cross_mappings(domain)\n    \n    # Generate domain-specific gates\n    generate_gates(domain)\n    \n    # Create domain templates\n    create_templates(domain)\n    \n    # Update system knowledge\n    update_knowledge_base(domain)\n    \n    return domain\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📊 Cross-Domain Impact Matrix\n\n### Impact Scoring\n- **High Impact (3):** Significant effect, requires coordination\n- **Medium Impact (2):** Moderate effect, needs consideration\n- **Low Impact (1):** Minor effect, awareness needed\n- **No Impact (0):** No direct effect\n\n### Matrix Template\n```\n           | Bus | Eng | Fin | Leg | Ops | Mkt | HR  | Sal | Prd |\n-----------|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|\nBusiness   |  -  |  3  |  3  |  2  |  3  |  3  |  2  |  3  |  3  |\nEngineering|  3  |  -  |  2  |  2  |  3  |  1  |  1  |  1  |  3  |\nFinancial  |  3  |  2  |  -  |  3  |  2  |  2  |  2  |  2  |  2  |\nLegal      |  2  |  2  |  3  |  -  |  2  |  2  |  3  |  2  |  2  |\nOperations |  3  |  3  |  2  |  2  |  -  |  1  |  2  |  2  |  2  |\nMarketing  |  3  |  1  |  2  |  2  |  1  |  -  |  1  |  3  |  3  |\nHR         |  2  |  1  |  2  |  3  |  2  |  1  |  -  |  2  |  2  |\nSales      |  3  |  1  |  2  |  2  |  2  |  3  |  2  |  -  |  3  |\nProduct    |  3  |  3  |  2  |  2  |  2  |  3  |  2  |  3  |  -  |\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Example: Generative Domain Creation\n\n### Scenario: "AI-Powered Sustainable Supply Chain"\n\n**Step 1: Analysis**\n- Doesn\'t fit cleanly into Operations (too AI-focused)\n- Doesn\'t fit cleanly into Engineering (too business-focused)\n- Sustainability aspect is unique\n- AI component is emerging technology\n\n**Step 2: Template Selection**\n- Choose: Hybrid Domain + Emerging Technology\n\n**Step 3: Questions Generated**\n1. What AI technologies will be used? (ML, optimization, prediction)\n2. What sustainability metrics matter? (Carbon footprint, waste reduction)\n3. What supply chain processes are targeted? (Procurement, logistics, inventory)\n4. What are the data requirements? (Real-time tracking, historical data)\n5. What are the integration points? (ERP, WMS, TMS systems)\n6. What are the regulatory requirements? (Environmental compliance)\n7. What are the cost implications? (AI infrastructure, training)\n8. What expertise is needed? (Data scientists, supply chain experts)\n\n**Step 4: Domain Synthesis**\n```yaml\ndomain_name: "AI-Powered Sustainable Supply Chain"\npurpose: "Optimize supply chain operations using AI while minimizing environmental impact"\n\nsub_domains:\n  - AI/ML Operations\n  - Sustainability Metrics\n  - Supply Chain Optimization\n  - Environmental Compliance\n  - Data Analytics\n\ncross_domain_impacts:\n  business: "New competitive advantage, sustainability positioning"\n  engineering: "AI infrastructure, data pipelines, integration"\n  financial: "AI costs, sustainability ROI, carbon credits"\n  legal: "Environmental regulations, data privacy"\n  operations: "Process changes, new workflows, monitoring"\n  marketing: "Sustainability messaging, green credentials"\n  hr: "New skills needed, training programs"\n  sales: "Sustainability as selling point"\n  product: "Sustainable product design, packaging"\n\nconstraints:\n  - Real-time data availability\n  - AI model accuracy requirements\n  - Sustainability certification standards\n  - Budget for AI infrastructure\n  - Timeline for implementation\n\ngates:\n  - Data Quality Gate (>95% accuracy)\n  - Sustainability Metrics Gate (measurable improvement)\n  - AI Model Performance Gate (>90% prediction accuracy)\n  - Integration Gate (seamless system integration)\n  - Compliance Gate (meets environmental standards)\n```\n\n**Step 5: System Integration**\n- Added to domain taxonomy\n- Cross-domain impacts mapped\n- Gates generated\n- Templates created for similar requests\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 Implementation in Murphy System\n\n### Backend Integration\n```python\n# murphy_complete_backend.py\n\nclass GenerativeDomainEngine:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.templates = load_templates()\n        self.existing_domains = load_domains()\n        self.question_framework = load_questions()\n    \n    async def process_request(self, request):\n        # Analyze request\n        analysis = self.analyze_request(request)\n        \n        if analysis[\'coverage\'] < 0.7:\n            # Need generative domain\n            return await self.create_generative_domain(request)\n        else:\n            # Use existing domains\n            return analysis[\'matched_domains\']\n    \n    async def create_generative_domain(self, request):\n        # Select template\n        template = self.select_template(request)\n        \n        # Generate questions\n        questions = self.generate_questions(template, request)\n        \n        # Conduct Q&A (interactive with user)\n        responses = await self.conduct_qa(questions)\n        \n        # Synthesize domain\n        domain = self.synthesize_domain(template, responses)\n        \n        # Validate\n        if self.validate_domain(domain):\n            # Integrate into system\n            self.integrate_domain(domain)\n            return domain\n        else:\n            # Request more information\n            gaps = self.identify_gaps(domain)\n            return await self.fill_gaps(domain, gaps)\n```\n\n### Frontend Integration\n```javascript\n// murphy_complete_ui.html\n\nasync function handleGenerativeDomain(request) {\n    // Send request to backend\n    const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/analyze-domain`, {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ request })\n    });\n    \n    const result = await response.json();\n    \n    if (result.needs_generative) {\n        // Show generative domain wizard\n        showGenerativeDomainWizard(result.questions);\n    } else {\n        // Use existing domains\n        applyDomains(result.domains);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showGenerativeDomainWizard(questions) {\n    // Create interactive Q&A interface\n    const wizard = createWizard(questions);\n    \n    // Collect responses\n    wizard.onComplete(async (responses) => {\n        // Send responses to backend\n        const domain = await synthesizeDomain(responses);\n        \n        // Show generated domain\n        displayGeneratedDomain(domain);\n        \n        // Ask for confirmation\n        confirmDomain(domain, (confirmed) => {\n            if (confirmed) {\n                integrateDomain(domain);\n            }\n        });\n    });\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📈 Benefits of This System\n\n### 1. def analyze_request(self, request: str) -> Dict:\n        """Analyze request and determine domain coverage"""\n        # Extract keywords\n        keywords = self._extract_keywords(request.lower())\n        \n        # Match against existing domains\n        domain_matches = {}\n        for domain_name, domain in self.domains.items():\n            score = self._calculate_domain_match(keywords, domain)\n            if score > 0:\n                domain_matches[domain_name] = score\n        \n        # Calculate coverage\n        total_score = sum(domain_matches.values())\n        coverage = min(total_score / 10.0, 1.0)  # Normalize to 0-1\n        \n        return {\n            \'coverage\': coverage,\n            \'matched_domains\': domain_matches,\n            \'needs_generative\': coverage < 0.7,\n            \'keywords\': keywords\n        }\n    \n    def _extract_keywords(self, text: str) -> List[str]:\n        """Extract relevant keywords from text"""\n        # Simple keyword extraction (can be enhanced with NLP)\n        domain_keywords = {\n            \'business\': [\'business\', \'strategy\', \'revenue\', \'growth\', \'market\', \'competitive\'],\n            \'engineering\': [\'technical\', \'engineering\', \'development\', \'architecture\', \'system\', \'software\'],\n            \'financial\': [\'financial\', \'budget\', \'cost\', \'roi\', \'investment\', \'accounting\'],\n            \'legal\': [\'legal\', \'compliance\', \'regulatory\', \'contract\', \'liability\', \'ip\'],\n            \'operations\': [\'operations\', \'process\', \'logistics\', \'supply chain\', \'quality\'],\n            \'marketing\': [\'marketing\', \'brand\', \'advertising\', \'campaign\', \'customer\'],\n            \'hr\': [\'hr\', \'hiring\', \'talent\', \'employee\', \'training\', \'compensation\'],\n            \'sales\': [\'sales\', \'revenue\', \'customer\', \'pricing\', \'channel\', \'account\'],\n            \'product\': [\'product\', \'feature\', \'roadmap\', \'user\', \'design\', \'ux\']\n        }\n        \n        found_keywords = []\n        for domain, keywords in domain_keywords.items():\n            for keyword in keywords:\n                if keyword in text:\n                    found_keywords.append(keyword)\n        \n        return found_keywords\n    \n    def _calculate_domain_match(self, keywords: List[str], domain: Domain) -> float:\n        """Calculate how well keywords match a domain"""\n        score = 0.0\n        domain_text = f"{domain.name} {domain.purpose} {\' \'.join(domain.sub_domains)}".lower()\n        \n        for keyword in keywords:\n            if keyword in domain_text:\n                score += 1.0\n        \n        return score\n    \n    def select_template(self, request: str, analysis: Dict) -> GenerativeDomainTemplate:\n        """Select appropriate template for generative domain"""\n        keywords = analysis[\'keywords\']\n        \n        # Check for industry-specific terms\n        industry_terms = [\'healthcare\', \'finance\', \'retail\', \'manufacturing\', \'education\']\n        if any(term in request.lower() for term in industry_terms):\n            return self.templates[\'industry\']\n        \n        # Check for multiple domain mentions\n        if len(analysis[\'matched_domains\']) >= 2:\n            return self.templates[\'hybrid\']\n        \n        # Check for technology terms\n        tech_terms = [\'ai\', \'ml\', \'blockchain\', \'iot\', \'cloud\', \'automation\']\n        if any(term in request.lower() for term in tech_terms):\n            return self.templates[\'technology\']\n        \n        # Default to process innovation\n        return self.templates[\'process\']\n    \n    def generate_questions(self, template: GenerativeDomainTemplate, request: str) -> List[Dict]:\n        """Generate questions for domain discovery"""\n        questions = []\n        \n        # Add template questions\n        for i, question in enumerate(template.discovery_questions):\n            questions.append({\n                \'id\': f\'q{i+1}\',\n                \'question\': question,\n                \'type\': \'text\',\n                \'required\': True\n            })\n        \n        # Add cross-domain impact questions\n        for domain_name in self.domains.keys():\n            questions.append({\n                \'id\': f\'impact_{domain_name}\',\n                \'question\': f\'How does this affect {domain_name}?\',\n                \'type\': \'text\',\n                \'required\': False\n            })\n        \n        return questions\n    \n    def synthesize_domain(self, template: GenerativeDomainTemplate, \n                         responses: Dict) -> Domain:\n        """Create new domain from template and responses"""\n        # Extract domain name\n        if template.template_type == \'industry\':\n            domain_name = responses.get(\'industry_name\', \'Custom\') + \' Domain\'\n        elif template.template_type == \'hybrid\':\n            domain_a = responses.get(\'primary_domain_a\', \'Domain A\')\n            domain_b = responses.get(\'primary_domain_b\', \'Domain B\')\n            domain_name = f"{domain_a} + {domain_b} Hybrid"\n        elif template.template_type == \'technology\':\n            domain_name = responses.get(\'technology_name\', \'Technology\') + \' Domain\'\n        else:\n            domain_name = responses.get(\'process_name\', \'Process\') + \' Innovation Domain\'\n        \n        # Extract purpose\n        purpose = responses.get(\'purpose\', \'Custom domain for specific requirements\')\n        \n        # Extract sub-domains\n        sub_domains = responses.get(\'sub_domains\', [])\n        if isinstance(sub_domains, str):\n            sub_domains = [s.strip() for s in sub_domains.split(\',\')]\n        \n        # Extract constraints\n        constraints = responses.get(\'constraints\', [])\n        if isinstance(constraints, str):\n            constraints = [c.strip() for c in constraints.split(\',\')]\n        \n        # Generate gates\n        gates = self._generate_domain_gates(domain_name, responses)\n        \n        # Build cross-impacts\n        cross_impacts = {}\n        for domain_name_key in self.domains.keys():\n            impact_key = f\'impact_{domain_name_key}\'\n            if impact_key in responses and responses[impact_key]:\n                cross_impacts[domain_name_key] = DomainImpact(\n                    target_domain=domain_name_key,\n                    impact_level=ImpactLevel.MEDIUM,  # Default, can be refined\n                    description=responses[impact_key],\n                    dependencies=[],\n                    constraints=[]\n                )\n        \n        # Create domain\n        domain = Domain(\n            name=domain_name,\n            domain_type=DomainType.GENERATIVE,\n            purpose=purpose,\n            sub_domains=sub_domains,\n            key_questions=template.discovery_questions,\n            cross_impacts=cross_impacts,\n            constraints=constraints,\n            gates=gates\n        )\n        \n        return domain\n    \n    def _generate_domain_gates(self, domain_name: str, responses: Dict) -> List[str]:\n        """Generate validation gates for domain"""\n        gates = [\n            f"{domain_name} Feasibility Gate",\n            f"{domain_name} Requirements Gate",\n            f"{domain_name} Validation Gate",\n            f"{domain_name} Compliance Gate"\n        ]\n        \n        # Add custom gates based on responses\n        if \'regulatory_requirements\' in responses:\n            gates.append(f"{domain_name} Regulatory Gate")\n        \n        if \'quality_standards\' in responses:\n            gates.append(f"{domain_name} Quality Gate")\n        \n        return gates\n    \n    def validate_domain(self, domain: Domain) -> Tuple[bool, List[str]]:\n        """Validate domain completeness"""\n        issues = []\n        \n        if not domain.name:\n            issues.append("Domain name is required")\n        \n        if not domain.purpose:\n            issues.append("Domain purpose is required")\n        \n        if len(domain.sub_domains) == 0:\n            issues.append("At least one sub-domain is required")\n        \n        if len(domain.key_questions) == 0:\n            issues.append("Key questions are required")\n        \n        if len(domain.gates) == 0:\n            issues.append("At least one gate is required")\n        \n        return len(issues) == 0, issues\n    \n    def integrate_domain(self, domain: Domain) -> bool:\n        """Integrate new domain into system"""\n        # Add to generative domains\n        domain_key = domain.name.lower().replace(\' \', \'_\')\n        self.generative_domains[domain_key] = domain\n        \n        # Update cross-impact matrix\n        self._update_impact_matrix(domain)\n        \n        return True\n    \n    def _update_impact_matrix(self, domain: Domain):\n        """Update cross-impact matrix with new domain"""\n        domain_key = domain.name.lower().replace(\' \', \'_\')\n        \n        # Add row for new domain\n        self.cross_impact_matrix[domain_key] = {}\n        \n        # Add impacts from new domain to existing domains\n        for target_domain, impact in domain.cross_impacts.items():\n            self.cross_impact_matrix[domain_key][target_domain] = impact.impact_level\n        \n        # Add impacts from existing domains to new domain (default to MEDIUM)\n        for existing_domain in self.domains.keys():\n            if existing_domain not in self.cross_impact_matrix:\n                self.cross_impact_matrix[existing_domain] = {}\n            self.cross_impact_matrix[existing_domain][domain_key] = ImpactLevel.MEDIUM\n    \n    def get_all_domains(self) -> List[Dict]:\n        """Get all domains (standard + generative)"""\n analysis"""\n        analysis = {\n            \'domains\': domain_names,\n            \'impacts\': {},\n            \'high_impact_pairs\': [],\n            \'dependencies\': []\n        }\n        \n              \n                    if impact == ImpactLevel.HIGH:\n                        analysis[\'high_impact_pairs\'].append({\n                            \'source\': source,\n Sales Strategy, Account Management, Channel Management\n   - Cross-impacts: HIGH on Business, Marketing, Product\n\n9. **Product Domain**\n   - Product Strategy, Development, Design, UX, Roadmap Planning\n   - Cross-impacts: HIGH on Business, Engineering, Marketing, Sales\n\n---\n\n### 2. **Generative Domain System** ✅\n\n#### 4 Domain Templates Created:\n\n**Template 1: New Industry Vertical**\n- For industry-specific requirements (Healthcare, Finance, Retail, etc.)\n- 8 discovery questions\n- Auto-generates industry-specific sub-domains, constraints, and gates\n\n**Template 2: Hybrid Domain**\n- For requests spanning multiple domains\n- Identifies integration points and synergies\n- Resolves conflicting requirements\n- Maps combined domain impacts\n\n**Template 3: Emerging Technology**\n- For new technology adoption (AI, Blockchain, IoT, etc.)\n- Assesses maturity level and implementation challenges\n- Identifies expertise and infrastructure requirements\n- Calculates costs and ROI\n\n**Template 4: Process Innovation**\n- For novel approaches to business processes\n- Defines current vs. future state\n- Identifies benefits and risks\n- Plans implementation and change management\n\n---\n\n### 3. **Cross-Domain Impact Matrix** ✅\n\nComplete 9x9 impact matrix with scoring:\n- **HIGH (3):** Significant effect, requires coordination\n- **MEDIUM (2):** Moderate effect, needs consideration  \n- **LOW (1):** Minor effect, awareness needed\n- **NONE (0):** No direct effect\n\nExample impacts:\n- Business → Engineering: HIGH (3)\n- Business → Financial: HIGH (3)\n- Engineering → Product: HIGH (3)\n- Marketing → Sales: HIGH (3)\n- Legal → HR: HIGH (3)\n\n---\n\n### 4. **Question Framework** ✅\n\n7-Phase discovery process:\n1. **Domain Identification** - Classify the request\n2. **Scope Definition** - Define boundaries\n3. **Requirements Gathering** - Collect all requirements\n4. **Stakeholder Analysis** - Identify needs and concerns\n5. **Risk Assessment** - Evaluate all risk types\n6. **Success Criteria** - Define metrics and milestones\n7. **Cross-Domain Impact** - Map dependencies\n\nEach phase has 4-8 targeted questions.\n\n---\n\n### 5. **Domain Augmentation Process** ✅\n\n7-Step automated workflow:\n\n```\nStep 1: Request Analysis\n  ↓ Extract concepts, match domains, calculate coverage\nStep 2: Template Selection  \n  ↓ Choose appropriate template based on request type\nStep 3: Question Generation\n  ↓ Create context-specific questions\nStep 4: Interactive Q&A\n  ↓ Collect user responses with follow-ups\nStep 5: Domain Synthesis\n  ↓ Fill template, generate sub-domains, map impacts\nStep 6: Validation\n  ↓ Check completeness, consistency, impacts\nStep 7: System Integration\n  ↓ Add to taxonomy, update mappings, generate gates\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🔧 Technical Implementation\n\n### Backend: `domain_engine.py` (600+ lines)\n\n**Core Classes:**\n- `DomainType` - Enum for domain classification\n- `ImpactLevel` - Enum for impact scoring\n- `DomainImpact` - Cross-domain impact definition\n- `Domain` - Complete domain specification\n- `GenerativeDomainTemplate` - Template for new domains\n- `DomainEngine` - Main engine with all logic\n\n**Key Methods:**\n- `analyze_request()` - Analyze and classify requests\n- `select_template()` - Choose appropriate template\n- `generate_questions()` - Create discovery questions\n- `synthesize_domain()` - Build new domain from responses\n- `validate_domain()` - Ensure domain completeness\n- `integrate_domain()` - Add to system taxonomy\n- `get_cross_impact_analysis()` - Analyze domain interactions\n\n---\n\n### Backend Integration: `murphy_complete_backend.py`\n\n**New API Endpoints:**\n\n1. **GET /api/domains**\n   - Returns all available domains (standard + generative)\n   - Response: `{domains: [...]}`\n\n2. **POST /api/analyze-domain**\n   - Analyzes request and determines domain coverage\n   - Request: `{request: "text"}`\n   - Response: `{needs_generative, coverage, matched_domains, questions}`\n\n3. **POST /api/create-generative-domain**\n   - Creates new domain from template responses\n   - Request: `{template_type, responses}`\n   - Response: `{success, domain}` or `{success: false, issues}`\n\n4. **POST /api/cross-impact-analysis**\n   - Analyzes cross-domain impacts\n   - Request: `{domains: [...]}`\n   - Response: `{domains, impacts, high_impact_pairs, dependencies}`\n\n---\n\n## 📋 Example: Generative Domain Creation\n\n### Scenario: "AI-Powered Sustainable Supply Chain"\n\n**Step 1: Analysis**\n```json\n{\n  "coverage": 0.45,\n  "matched_domains": {\n    "operations": 2.0,\n    "engineering": 1.5\n  },\n  "needs_generative": true\n}\n```\n\n**Step 2: Template Selection**\n- Selected: Hybrid Domain + Emerging Technology\n\n**Step 3: Questions Generated**\n1. What AI technologies will be used?\n2. What sustainability metrics matter?\n3. What supply chain processes are targeted?\n4. What are the data requirements?\n5. What are the integration points?\n6. What are the regulatory requirements?\n7. What are the cost implications?\n8. What expertise is needed?\n\n**Step 4: Domain Synthesized**\n```yaml\ndomain_name: "AI-Powered Sustainable Supply Chain"\npurpose: "Optimize supply chain using AI while minimizing environmental impact"\n\nsub_domains:\n  - AI/ML Operations\n  - Sustainability Metrics\n  - Supply Chain Optimization\n  - Environmental Compliance\n  - Data Analytics\n\ncross_impacts:\n  business: "New competitive advantage, sustainability positioning"\n  engineering: "AI infrastructure, data pipelines, integration"\n  financial: "AI costs, sustainability ROI, carbon credits"\n  legal: "Environmental regulations, data privacy"\n  operations: "Process changes, new workflows, monitoring"\n  \nconstraints:\n  - Real-time data availability\n  - AI model accuracy requirements\n  - Sustainability certification standards\n  \ngates:\n  - Data Quality Gate (>95% accuracy)\n  - Sustainability Metrics Gate\n  - AI Model Performance Gate (>90% prediction)\n  - Integration Gate\n  - Compliance Gate\n```\n\n**Step 5: System Integration**\n- Added to domain taxonomy\n- Cross-impacts mapped to all 9 standard domains\n- Gates generated and activated\n- Template created for similar future requests\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Key Features\n\n### 1. **Automatic Domain Classification**\n- Analyzes any request text\n- Extracts relevant keywords\n- Matches against 9 standard domains\n- Calculates coverage score (0-1)\n- Determines if generative domain needed (<0.7 coverage)\n\n### 2. **Intelligent Template Selection**\n- Industry-specific terms → Industry Vertical template\n- Multiple domain mentions → Hybrid Domain template\n- Technology terms (AI, ML, IoT) → Emerging Technology template\n- Default → Process Innovation template\n\n### 3. **Dynamic Question Generation**\n- Template-based questions\n- Context-specific questions\n- Cross-domain impact questions\n- Follow-up questions based on responses\n\n### 4. **Domain Synthesis**\n- Fills template with user responses\n- Generates sub-domains automatically\n- Maps cross-domain impacts\n- Creates domain-specific constraints\n- Generates validation gates\n\n### 5. **Validation & Integration**\n- Checks domain completeness\n- Validates consistency\n- Verifies cross-domain impacts\n- Integrates into system taxonomy\n- Updates impact matrix\n\n---\n\n## 📊 Coverage Analysis\n\n### Standard Domains Coverage\n- ✅ Business (Meta-Domain) -
